<script>
P.when('tabela-manager').register('tabela-table-myitable', function(TabelaManager) {
    TabelaManager.create('myitable');
});
</script>

<script>
P.when('A',
        'tabela-manager',
        'tabela-history-handler-factory',
        'tabela-table-myitable',
        'ready')
    .execute('tabela-history-myitable', function(
         A,
         TabelaManager,
         tabelaHistoryHandlerFactory){

        var table = TabelaManager.get('myitable'),
        historyHandlers = [];
        
    
    historyHandlers.push(tabelaHistoryHandlerFactory.handlers['SORT'.toLowerCase()]);
    
    historyHandlers.push(tabelaHistoryHandlerFactory.handlers['SEARCH'.toLowerCase()]);
    
    historyHandlers.push(tabelaHistoryHandlerFactory.handlers['PAGINATION'.toLowerCase()]);
    
    
    table.setHistoryHandlers(historyHandlers, {
        'refresh' : 'false'
    });
});
</script>

<script>
	var delayedLoad = false;
	P.when('A').execute(function(A){
		
		A.on("tabela:load-delayed-rows", function(data) {
			delayedLoad = true;
			setClientState();
		});
	});
	
	P.when('tabela-manager').execute(function(TabelaManager){
		
		if( !delayedLoad )
		{
			setClientState();
		}
	});
	
	var setClientState = function()
	{
		TabelaManager.get('myitable').setClientState("recordsAboveTheFold", "10");
		TabelaManager.get('myitable').setClientState("confirmActionPageMaxRecords", "250");
		TabelaManager.get('myitable').setClientState("totalNumberOfRecords", "15");
		TabelaManager.get('myitable').setClientState("currentNumberOfRecords", "10");
		
			var viewId = 'FBA';
			TabelaManager.get('myitable').setClientState("viewId", viewId);
		
		
	}
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
    if (typeof P !== 'undefined') {
        P.when("A").execute(function (A) {
            A.on("a:dropdown:selected:language", function (data) {
                var language = data.value,
                        location = encodeURIComponent(window.location.href);

                if (language) {
                    window.location.href = "/gp/switch-language.html?formSubmitted=true&language=" + language + "&location=" + location;
                }
            });
        });
    }
</script>
